    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);

    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);

{
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;

    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat10_2.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_7.xy;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_7.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;

    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
    u_xlat6.x = clamp(u_xlat6.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat12 = -abs(u_xlat0.x) * abs(u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat16_3.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.x = abs(u_xlat0.x) * u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x + u_xlat12;
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_1.x / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat18;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_1.x = _Metallic;
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat10_2 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat10_2.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = (-u_xlat10_2.xyz) * u_xlat16_1.xxx + u_xlat10_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat10_2.w + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = _IFMask * u_xlat16_19 + 1.0;
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat6.xxx * u_xlat16_1.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat5.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat5.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * vec3(0.349999994, 0.349999994, 0.349999994);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat6.xyz * u_xlat5.xyz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz / u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_3;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xzw = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_10)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_4.z;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];

vec4 u_xlat0;

mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.w = 0.0;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);

    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;

    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;

    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;

    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_3;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xzw = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_10)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_4.z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_2.w + _RoughNessOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_3.x = min(max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_9.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_9.xy;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;

    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;

    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat10.x = -abs(u_xlat2.x) * abs(u_xlat2.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat16_3.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_1.x * abs(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x + u_xlat10.x;
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_1.x / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat18;

    u_xlat16_1.x = _Metallic;

#else

    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);

    u_xlatb26 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb26 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb29 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb29 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb26 = u_xlatb26 || u_xlatb29;

    u_xlat26 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat26 = min(max(u_xlat26, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat26 = clamp(u_xlat26, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat26);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_25) + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_0.y * u_xlat16_0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_0.x + (-u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_3 = u_xlat16_0.yzzx * u_xlat16_0.xyzz;

    u_xlat16_7.y = dot(unity_SHBg, u_xlat16_3);

    u_xlat16_28 = max(u_xlat16_28, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.25);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = max(u_xlat16_4.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_25 * u_xlat16_4.x + u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_25) + u_xlat2.xyz;

    u_xlat5.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat5.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;

    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;

#endif

    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_2.w + _RoughNessOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_3.x = min(max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_9.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_9.xy;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_0.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat10.x = -abs(u_xlat2.x) * abs(u_xlat2.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat16_3.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_1.x * abs(u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x + u_xlat10.x;
    u_xlat2.x = max(u_xlat2.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat16_1.x / u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat2.x * u_xlat2.x;

#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);

#else

    u_xlatb29 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb29 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb26 = u_xlatb26 || u_xlatb29;
    u_xlat16_25 = (u_xlatb26) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_25;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_25) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat26 = dot(u_xlat16_0.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat26 = min(max(u_xlat26, 0.0), 1.0);
#else

#endif

    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_25) + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_0.y * u_xlat16_0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_0.x * u_xlat16_0.x + (-u_xlat16_4.x);

    u_xlat16_7.y = dot(unity_Builtins2Array[u_xlati26 / 7].unity_SHAgArray, u_xlat16_0);

    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.25);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz + u_xlat16_7.xyz;

    u_xlat16_4.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_25 = u_xlat16_25 * u_xlat16_4.x + u_xlat16_28;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_25) + u_xlat2.xyz;

    u_xlat5.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat5.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;

    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _Cutoff;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _NormalStrong;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _IFMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RenderType;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SpecularColor;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD9;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD10;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD11;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
vec3 u_xlat3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump float u_xlat16_10;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _UVScallePaner.xy + _UVScallePaner.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.w = 0.0;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat0.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat0.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = (-u_xlat1.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = dot(u_xlat0.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = min(max(vs_TEXCOORD0.z, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    vs_TEXCOORD0.z = clamp(vs_TEXCOORD0.z, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD1.xy = in_TEXCOORD1.xy * unity_LightmapST.xy + unity_LightmapST.zw;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyw = u_xlat3.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.w = u_xlat16_3.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3.w = u_xlat16_3.y;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _MainLightPosition.xyz + _MainHighLightOffset.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_22 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(_MainLightPosition.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_4.x);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xxx * _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat16_3;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD6.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat5.x = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[0].z;
    u_xlat5.y = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[1].z;
    u_xlat5.z = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixV[2].z;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat5.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat16_4.xzw = u_xlat16_4.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xxx + _DarkCorner.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = (-vec3(u_xlat16_10)) * _DarkCorner.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xzw;
    vs_TEXCOORD6.w = u_xlat16_4.x;
    u_xlat2.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = u_xlat16_4.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.w = u_xlat16_4.z;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat0.zxy * u_xlat2.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.yzx * u_xlat2.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    vs_TEXCOORD9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD10 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD11 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat1.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat1.xxxx + u_xlat0;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat1.zzzz + u_xlat0;
    gl_Position = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    return;
}

in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD2;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
vec3 u_xlat6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
float u_xlat14;
float u_xlat21;
mediump float u_xlat16_22;
void main()
{
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.x;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.x;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.x;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _NormalStrong;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_2.w + _RoughNessOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_3.x = min(max(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_3.x = clamp(u_xlat16_3.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_8.xy = u_xlat16_1.xx * u_xlat16_8.xy;
    u_xlat16_4.x = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.y;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.y;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.y;
    u_xlat16_4.y = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = vs_TEXCOORD8.z;
    u_xlat0.y = vs_TEXCOORD9.z;
    u_xlat0.z = vs_TEXCOORD6.z;
    u_xlat16_4.z = dot(u_xlat16_8.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_1.x);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz);
    u_xlat7.x = -abs(u_xlat0.x) * abs(u_xlat0.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat16_3.x * u_xlat16_3.x;
    u_xlat14 = u_xlat16_3.x * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.x = abs(u_xlat0.x) * u_xlat16_22;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x + u_xlat7.x;
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 0.00100000005);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_22 / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat14;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat16_22 = _Metallic;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_22 = min(max(u_xlat16_22, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_22 = clamp(u_xlat16_22, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz + vec3(-0.0399999991, -0.0399999991, -0.0399999991);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_22) * u_xlat7.xyz + vec3(0.0399999991, 0.0399999991, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-u_xlat16_2.xyz) * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat16_2.w + -1.0;
    SV_Target0.w = _IFMask * u_xlat16_22 + 1.0;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _GISpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD2.w;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(0.349999994, 0.349999994, 0.349999994);
    u_xlat16_4 = texture(unity_Lightmap, vs_TEXCOORD1.xy);
    u_xlat16_22 = u_xlat16_4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * vec3(4.84000015, 4.84000015, 4.84000015);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat21 = min(max(u_xlat21, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat21 = clamp(u_xlat21, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.y * 0.5 + 0.75;
    u_xlat16_1.x = max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.5);
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(u_xlat16_1.x, 1.25);
    u_xlat6.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat2.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_22) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.x = (-u_xlat16_1.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_22 * u_xlat16_8.x + u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = _GIDiffuseColor.xyz + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.x = vs_TEXCOORD6.w;
    u_xlat2.y = vs_TEXCOORD8.w;
    u_xlat2.z = vs_TEXCOORD9.w;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz * _ExposureColor.xyz + vec3(0.155000001, 0.155000001, 0.155000001);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz / u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(1.01900005, 1.01900005, 1.01900005);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = log2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.20000005, 2.20000005, 2.20000005);
    SV_Target0.xyz = exp2(u_xlat16_1.xyz);
    return;
}

  Name "ShadowCaster"

"// hash: 7e1f6e5f7ab0171f
#ifdef VERTEX
#version 100

uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[4];
uniform 	vec4 hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[4];
uniform 	vec4 _ShadowBias;
uniform 	mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
uniform 	vec3 _LightDirection;
attribute highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
attribute highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
attribute highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
varying highp vec2 vs_TEXCOORD0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);

    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
